### Test Three
* Sell when the price hits the lower line of the 20p 2std bollinger
* No Stoploss
* Results:
```
Total Trades: 148
Percent Up: 16.89
Percent Down: 83.11
Total Points Moved Down: 402.00
Potential Profit: 201000.00
```
